< Review>
I had called a different dental office in the area before Arch Dental and that other office did not make any effort whatsoever to find me an appointment window that worked best for my schedule. They claimed they couldn't schedule me anytime soon and they don't schedule too far in advance. I cannot say this with certainty but I believe they were treating me like this due to my less desirable HMO plan.

Luckily, I decided to call Arch Dental and was offered an appointment window of my choosing. The entire staff was welcoming during my first visit especially the dental assistant, Yvonne, who took my X-rays. Dr. Kaur was also great in her work as I did not feel any extreme discomfort during the cleaning. Most importantly, I was glad that they did not make up an excuse to charge me anything for my free 6-month cleaning.

If everything goes well with my future visits, then Dr. Kaur will probably become my long-term dentist.< /Review>

Very nice people.
I'm a crotchety old geezer type.  Think of the old men up in the balcony on the Muppets, and you've got me pegged pretty good.

These young women are amazingly patient, and forgiving.  They put up with my nonsense, bad behavior, bad humour, for quite a while;  and
they keep inviting me back and encouraging me to take better care of my teeth.

What have I had done.  A couple of cleanings,  a couple of fillings, an old  crown redone.  The initial discussion on a series of implants.  Sent out to a specialist to have a bone graft done for the implants.

And all this time, Dr. Kaur and her wonderful team have been just amazingly patient, and wonderfully cheerful and encouraging.

I can honestly say that I would recommend them to all my family and friends;  without any reservations.

John Willis        August 9th  2017< /review>

< text>
This place was a bust for me.  The meal started out well.  Arugula, beet and Gorgonzola cheese salad; all things I like.  The bread had rosemary in it and it could have been baked on site, good.  For my entry I had something from their special menu.  Lamb and pasta with red sauce.  This last thing turned me off.  First was the lamb, what little there was of it was not good, and I usually love lamb.  The pieces were fatty and chewy.  The pasta came out of a box.  But beyond all of this, it was swimming in sauce, see picture.  The other thing that turned me off was there was a large party celebrating a birthday (about 20 folks) and they all had to pass by me and hit the rest room, before heading out.

The service itself was fine, despite having to wait on the 20 some crew.  There was only one guy cooking and he was putting together the salads and everything else and getting it out in a timely manner.  The restaurant space is small; very narrow space but deep.<//text>

I had the crab canaloni; the lobster sauce was the best I have had, the portion was huge as well and for only $13.00...  My husband had the fettuccini alfredo and shared a lemon tart both tasted amazing.

< Review>
I had a guest meet me for dinner here 5-19-2021.  Both of us left pretty disappointed because of the food.  The breading on the chicken piccata was mushy; the sauce was more of a capellini soup.  I order this dish from every restaurant when it's offered‚Äì it's a favorite.  I didn't even finish my meal.  My guest was disappointed in bland seasoning for his seafood dish in a tomato sauce.  He had to add a generous amount of salt and pepper so that it had any flavor (he said to me as he dumped it in). The service was decent; it was hilarious to see "20%, 30%, 40%" as options for a gratuity.  Service was 18% worthy, as items were forgotten and the entire time the server had to keep running back and forth.  My guest finished his gorgonzola salad before the extra dressing was delivered.  The bruschetta was good.  Sadly the flavors of the meals just don't do the photos of menu items justice (online).  I chose this restaurant because a friend once worked here.  We have no plans to return.</Review>

They are always friendly & helpful! We moved to the area about 2 years ago & chose this location because it was indoors, not too far from home, has convenient hours, and it is clean. It took us a while to decide where to store our household goods since we moved into a smaller house from out-of-state.  We are very happy that we chose this location!  All of the storage facilities closer to our house were not climate controlled, cost more & usually drive-up type.  (We had a drive up storage in Spokane & although it can be easier, it was humid & musky even though it was a brand new facility. Plus we had so many bugs at that one!) I will definitely chose indoor facilities from now on, just like this one!!!

Adie has been there to help us out since we started.  They contacted us at the first sign of something possibly leaking by our unit, luckily nothing was damaged or leaking inside, but it is good to know they actually take a look at things!  It is easy to drive up close to get things in & out.  They offer carts free of charge to use which is very helpful, I use them almost every time I go there. Every associate has always been helpful & courteous.

It is located right off of the 405, close to shopping & not far from my husband's job.  It is never too crowded to find close parking.  I would recommend this location!< /Review>

<Resp>None< /Resp>< Review>
I am very disappointed in my experience here. When I got my storage, I was not told that in 6 months, the price would increase 20%, which is almost a $60 increase for my storage unit. I've rented many storages in the past, including a different Public Storage, and I've never experienced this. Some storages such as U-Haul actually decreased the rate after a certain period as an incentive to keep customers who pay on time. When I called the corporate office to express my concerns, the representative told me that the contract I signed says, "subject to change" and therefore they are able to make an "executive decision" to raise rates 20%. This forces many customers to downsize (where the price will again increase in 6 months) or pay the higher rate, as it is a huge hassle to rent a truck and movers to move to a new storage. I feel that this practice is very unethical. I would not recommend this storage - there are many nice storages in the Gardena/ Redondo Beach area without this policy. It may also be helpful to look at the reviews of this storage on Yelp.</Review>

< review>
When I signed up for this storage space at the end of 2011 it was the best deal in the area.  I haven't priced units recently so I don't know if the price is still competitive.
I have a space on the 3rd floor.  Sometimes I have problems accessing the elevator but it just means having to input my password 2 or 3 times.
The bathroom on the 3rd floor does not work - it has not worked since I moved in.
There are no trash cans available, either.
I understand Public Storage might be concerned about a) the customers destroying the restroom, and b) dealing with dumping problems, but isn't that part of the business?
Adie is the manager in the office and has been there since I began renting while all the other employees have come and gone.  I hope Public Storage is paying her a decent wage because she deserves it!</review>

< Review>
Last year, when I was in need of a storage space, I had actually already reserved a space elsewhere when I happened to drive by the Public Storage on 190th St.  On a whim, I stopped by "just to see" what they had to offer.  Adie was the one who greeted me & enthusiastically shared information about their facility. It just so happened that there was a space available in a terrific location, too. I signed up immediately & cancelled my other reservation.  I have been completely happy w/this decision.  The staff is the BEST.  Always friendly & helpful!  The place sparkles w/their care.  Victor (also always smiling & friendly!) was polishing the elevator when I was there last week!  They all work very hard to keep the place spic & span!  The place is well-lit, temperature-controlled, & completely clean.  There are carts available (free rental) to ferry boxes & heavy items to your storage space.  There is also a nice restroom facility, & the office has packing materials for purchase.  It is the best place to store your things!  But the icing on the cake is the terrific staff who are always kind, caring, & helpful.  Heartwarming!  (P.S.  I stopped by there last week, & Adie knew me by name & my space number instantly, even though I had not seen her in a few months.  Talk about great customer service!!  She is amazing!)</Review>

Andrea and Mike were the example of quality customer service. Thank you for exemplifying the Twelve Best Practices of Customer Service.

"The twelve best practices are found in companies that exemplify excellent customer service. These practices are not just something the company does, the practices are the company. Every employee in the company must understand and carry out these practices on a daily basis. Hiring people with the right attitudes and keeping them constantly trained, rewarded and recognized for demonstrating the best of these twelve practices is the way that companies achieve success. It is essential that the top person in the organization, CEO or owner also demonstrate these practices; not just among external customers, but among those internal customers, especially employees. Remembering that happy employees make happy customers is a critical bit of advice for every chief executive."

Richard C. Whiteley, The Forum Corporation, 1991< /Review>
